# MovieTicketing Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                      | Function Name          | HTTP Method | Template Rendered          | Context Variables Passed to Template                             |
|--------------------------------|------------------------|-------------|----------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------| 
| /                              | root_redirect          | GET         | N/A (redirect)             | N/A                                                             |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard_page         | GET         | dashboard.html             | featured_movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, rating:float), upcoming_releases (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies                       | movie_catalog          | GET         | movie_catalog.html         | movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, poster_url:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>        | movie_details          | GET         | movie_details.html         | movie (dict: movie_id:int, title:str, director:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, description:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>/showtimes | showtime_selection    | GET         | showtime_selection.html    | showtimes (list of dict: showtime_id:int, date:str, time:str, theater_name:str, price:float), theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str), filter_theater_id (int or None), filter_date (str or None) |
| /showtimes/select/<int:showtime_id> | select_showtime     | POST        | redirect to seat_selection.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /seat-selection/<int:showtime_id> | seat_selection      | GET         | seat_selection.html        | seat_map (list of dict: seat_id:int, row:str, column:int, seat_type:str, status:str), selected_seats (list of str seat IDs), showtime_id (int) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | booking_confirmation | GET         | booking_confirmation.html  | showtime (dict: showtime_id:int, movie_title:str, theater_name:str, date:str, time:str, price:float), selected_seats (list of str), total_price (float) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | confirm_booking      | POST        | redirect to booking_history.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /bookings                    | booking_history        | GET         | booking_history.html       | bookings (list of dict: booking_id:int, movie_title:str, booking_date:str, seats_booked:list of str, status:str) |
| /bookings/<int:booking_id>    | booking_details        | GET         | booking_details.html       | booking (dict: booking_id:int, showtime_id:int, customer_name:str, customer_email:str, booking_date:str, total_price:float, status:str, seats_booked:list of str) |
| /theaters                    | theater_information    | GET         | theater_information.html   | theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str, location:str, city:str, screens:int, facilities:str), filter_location (str or None) |

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Elements:
  - ID: dashboard-page (Div) - Container for the dashboard page.
  - ID: featured-movies (Div) - Displays featured movie recommendations.
  - ID: browse-movies-button (Button) - Navigates to movie_catalog route (movie_catalog).
  - ID: view-bookings-button (Button) - Navigates to booking_history route (booking_history).
  - ID: showtimes-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection root (redirect to /showtimes or dashboard to showtimes function).

### 2. templates/movie_catalog.html
- Page Title: Movie Catalog
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Catalog
- Elements:
  - ID: catalog-page (Div) - Container for the catalog page.
  - ID: search-input (Input) - Text field to search movies.
  - ID: genre-filter (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter movies by genre.
  - ID: movies-grid (Div) - Grid displaying movie cards.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-movie-button-{movie_id} (Button) - Button on each movie card to view details, navigates to movie_details with movie_id.

### 3. templates/movie_details.html
- Page Title: Movie Details
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Details
- Elements:
  - ID: movie-details-page (Div) - Container for movie details.
  - ID: movie-title (H1) - Displays the movie title.
  - ID: movie-director (Div) - Displays the movie director.
  - ID: movie-rating (Div) - Displays the movie rating.
  - ID: movie-description (Div) - Displays the movie description.
  - ID: select-showtime-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection for this movie.

### 4. templates/showtime_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Showtime
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Showtime
- Elements:
  - ID: showtime-page (Div) - Container for the showtime selection page.
  - ID: showtimes-list (Div) - List of available showtimes.
  - ID: theater-filter (Dropdown) - Filter showtimes by theater.
  - ID: date-filter (Input) - Filter showtimes by date.
  - Dynamic Button ID: select-showtime-button-{showtime_id} (Button) - Button to select a showtime, posts to select_showtime route.

### 5. templates/seat_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Seats
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Seats
- Elements:
  - ID: seat-selection-page (Div) - Container for seat selection.
  - ID: seat-map (Div) - Interactive seat map.
  - ID: selected-seats-display (Div) - Shows selected seats.
  - Dynamic Button ID: seat-{row}{col} (Button) - Each seat button for seat selection.
  - ID: proceed-booking-button (Button) - Proceeds to booking confirmation.

### 6. templates/booking_confirmation.html
- Page Title: Booking Confirmation
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking Confirmation
- Elements:
  - ID: confirmation-page (Div) - Container for confirmation details.
  - ID: booking-summary (Div) - Summary of the booking.
  - ID: customer-name (Input) - Input field for customer name.
  - ID: customer-email (Input) - Input field for customer email.
  - ID: confirm-booking-button (Button) - Confirms booking submission.

### 7. templates/booking_history.html
- Page Title: Booking History
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking History
- Elements:
  - ID: bookings-page (Div) - Container for booking history.
  - ID: bookings-table (Table) - Displays all bookings.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-booking-button-{booking_id} (Button) - To view individual booking details.
  - ID: status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter bookings by status.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.

### 8. templates/theater_information.html
- Page Title: Theater Information
- Main Heading (<h1>): Theater Information
- Elements:
  - ID: theater-page (Div) - Container for theater info.
  - ID: theaters-list (Div) - Displays list of theaters.
  - ID: theater-location-filter (Dropdown) - Filter theaters by location.
  - ID: facilities-display (Div) - Shows facilities of selected theater.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.


Navigation Summary:
- dashboard_page -> movie_catalog (browse-movies-button)
- dashboard_page -> booking_history (view-bookings-button)
- dashboard_page -> showtime_selection or showtimes page (showtimes-button)
- movie_catalog -> movie_details (view-movie-button-{movie_id})
- movie_details -> showtime_selection (select-showtime-button)
- showtime_selection -> seat_selection (select-showtime-button-{showtime_id})
- seat_selection -> booking_confirmation (proceed-booking-button)
- booking_confirmation -> booking_history (confirm-booking-button)
- booking_history -> booking_details (view-booking-button-{booking_id})
- booking_history -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)
- theater_information -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/movies.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date
- Description: Stores movie information.
- Example Rows:
  1|The Matrix|Lana Wachowski|Action|8.7|136|A computer hacker learns about the true nature of reality and his role in the war against its controllers.|1999-03-31
  2|Inception|Christopher Nolan|Sci-Fi|8.8|148|A skilled thief who steals corporate secrets through the use of dream-sharing technology is given the inverse task of planting an idea.|2010-07-16
  3|The Shawshank Redemption|Frank Darabont|Drama|9.3|142|Two imprisoned men bond over a number of years, finding solace and eventual redemption through acts of common decency.|1994-09-23

### 2. data/theaters.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities
- Description: Stores theater information.
- Example Rows:
  1|Cinema Max|123 Main St|New York|10|IMAX, Dolby, Wheelchair Access
  2|Galaxy Cinemas|456 Broadway|Los Angeles|8|3D, Premium Sound, Parking
  3|Starlight Theater|789 Park Ave|Chicago|6|Luxury Seating, Restaurant, VIP Lounge

### 3. data/showtimes.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats
- Description: Stores showtimes for movies at theaters.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|19:00|12.99|85
  2|1|1|2025-02-01|22:30|12.99|40
  3|2|2|2025-02-01|18:00|14.99|95

### 4. data/seats.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status
- Description: Stores seat information and booking status.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|A|1|Standard|Available
  2|1|1|A|2|Standard|Available
  3|1|1|B|5|Premium|Booked

### 5. data/bookings.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked
- Description: Stores user bookings.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|John Doe|john@example.com|2025-01-15|25.98|Confirmed|A1,A2
  2|2|Jane Smith|jane@example.com|2025-01-16|12.99|Confirmed|F10
  3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@example.com|2025-01-17|29.98|Confirmed|C3,C4

### 6. data/genres.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): genre_id|genre_name|description
- Description: Stores genre metadata.
- Example Rows:
  1|Action|Fast-paced movies with exciting sequences and combat
  2|Drama|Character-driven stories exploring complex themes
  3|Sci-Fi|Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts

---

This design specification details all Flask routes, HTML templates, and data file schemas required to enable parallel development of backend and frontend for the MovieTicketing application. All names, types, and IDs are consistent across sections.

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <title>Booking Confirmation</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1 id="booking-confirmation-title">Booking Confirmation</h1>
    <div id="confirmation-page">
        <div id="booking-summary">
            <div>Movie: {{ showtime.movie_title }}</div>
            <div>Theater: {{ showtime.theater_name }}</div>
            <div>Date: {{ showtime.date }}</div>
            <div>Time: {{ showtime.time }}</div>
            <div>Price: ${{ showtime.price }}</div>
            <div id="selected-seats-display">Selected Seats: {% for seat in selected_seats %}{{ seat }} {% endfor %}</div>
            <div>Total Price: ${{ total_price }}</div>
        </div>
        <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('confirm_booking', showtime_id=showtime.showtime_id) }}">
            <label for="customer-name">Name:</label>
            <input type="text" id="customer-name" name="customer_name" required />
            <label for="customer-email">Email:</label>
            <input type="email" id="customer-email" name="customer_email" required />
            <button id="confirm-booking-button" type="submit">Confirm Booking</button>
        </form>
    </div>
    <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard_page') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
</body>
</html>

customer_email:str, booking_date:str, total_price:float, status:str, seats_booked:list of str) | | /theaters                    | theater_information    | GET         | theater_information.html   | for the showtime selection page.   - ID: showtimes-list (Div) - List of available showtimes.   - ID: theater-filter (Dropdown) - Filter showtimes by theater.   - ID: date-filter (Input) - Filter showtimes by date.   - Dynamic Button ID: select-showtime-button-{showtime_id} (Button) - Button to select a showtime, posts to select_showtime route.  ### 5. templates/seat_selection.html - Page Title: Select Seats - Main Heading (<h1>): Select Seats - Elements:   - ID: seat-selection-page (Div) - Container for seat selection.   - ID: seat-map (Div) - Interactive seat map.   - ID: selected-seats-display (Div) - Shows selected seats.   - Dynamic Button ID: seat-{row}{col} (Button) - Each seat button for seat selection.   - ID: proceed-booking-button (Button) - Proceeds to booking confirmation.  ### 6. templates/booking_confirmation.html - Page Title: Booking Confirmation - Main Heading (<h1>): Booking Confirmation - Elements:   - ID: confirmation-page (Div) - Container for confirmation details.   - ID: booking-summary (Div) - Summary of the booking.   - ID: customer-name (Input) - Input field for customer name.   - ID: customer-email (Input) - Input field for customer email.   - ID: confirm-booking-button (Button) - Confirms booking submission.  ### 7. templates/booking_history.html - Page Title: Booking History - Main Heading (<h1>): Booking History - Elements:   - ID: bookings-page (Div) - Container for booking history.   - ID: bookings-table (Table) - Displays all bookings.   - Dynamic Button ID: view-booking-button-{booking_id} (Button) - To view individual booking details.   - ID: status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter bookings by status.   - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.  ### 8. theaters-list (Div) - Displays list of theaters.   - ID: theater-location-filter (Dropdown) - Filter theaters by location.   - ID: facilities-display (Div) - Shows facilities of selected theater.   - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.   Navigation Summary: - dashboard_page -> movie_catalog (browse-movies-button) - dashboard_page -> booking_history (view-bookings-button) - dashboard_page -> showtime_selection or showtimes page (showtimes-button) - movie_catalog -> movie_details (view-movie-button-{movie_id}) - movie_details -> showtime_selection (select-showtime-button) - showtime_selection -> seat_selection (select-showtime-button-{showtime_id}) - seat_selection -> booking_confirmation (proceed-booking-button) - booking_confirmation -> booking_history (confirm-booking-button) - booking_history -> booking_details (view-booking-button-{booking_id}) - booking_history -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard) - theater_information -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)  ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas  ### 1. data/movies.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date - Description: Stores movie information. - Example Rows:   1|The Matrix|Lana Wachowski|Action|8.7|136|A computer hacker learns about the true nature of reality and his role in the war against its controllers.|1999-03-31   2|Inception|Christopher Nolan|Sci-Fi|8.8|148|A skilled thief who steals corporate secrets through the use of dream-sharing technology is given the inverse task of planting an idea.|2010-07-16   3|The Shawshank Redemption|Frank Darabont|Drama|9.3|142|Two imprisoned men bond over a number of years, finding solace and eventual redemption through acts of common decency.|1994-09-23  ### 2. data/theaters.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities - Description: Stores theater information. - Example Rows:   1|Cinema Max|123 Main St|New York|10|IMAX, Dolby, Wheelchair Access   2|Galaxy Cinemas|456 Broadway|Los Angeles|8|3D, Premium Sound, Parking   3|Starlight Theater|789 Park Ave|Chicago|6|Luxury Seating, Restaurant, VIP Lounge  ### 3. data/showtimes.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats - Description: Stores showtimes for movies at theaters. - Example Rows:   1|1|1|2025-02-01|19:00|12.99|85   2|1|1|2025-02-01|22:30|12.99|40   3|2|2|2025-02-01|18:00|14.99|95  ### 4. data/seats.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status - Description: Stores seat information and booking status. - Example Rows:   1|1|1|A|1|Standard|Available   2|1|1|A|2|Standard|Available   3|1|1|B|5|Premium|Booked  ### 5. data/bookings.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked - Description: Stores user bookings. - Example Rows:   1|1|John Doe|john@example.com|2025-01-15|25.98|Confirmed|A1,A2   2|2|Jane Smith|jane@example.com|2025-01-16|12.99|Confirmed|F10   3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@example.com|2025-01-17|29.98|Confirmed|C3,C4  ### 6. data/genres.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): genre_id|genre_name|description - Description: Stores genre metadata. - Example Rows:   1|Action|Fast-paced movies with exciting sequences and combat   2|Drama|Character-driven stories exploring complex themes   3|Sci-Fi|Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts  ---  This design specification details all Flask routes, HTML templates, and data file schemas required to enable parallel development of backend and frontend for the MovieTicketing application. All names, types, and IDs are consistent across sections.

# MovieTicketing Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                      | Function Name          | HTTP Method | Template Rendered          | Context Variables Passed to Template                             |
|--------------------------------|------------------------|-------------|----------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------| 
| /                              | root_redirect          | GET         | N/A (redirect)             | N/A                                                             |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard_page         | GET         | dashboard.html             | featured_movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, rating:float), upcoming_releases (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies                       | movie_catalog          | GET         | movie_catalog.html         | movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, poster_url:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>        | movie_details          | GET         | movie_details.html         | movie (dict: movie_id:int, title:str, director:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, description:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>/showtimes | showtime_selection    | GET         | showtime_selection.html    | showtimes (list of dict: showtime_id:int, date:str, time:str, theater_name:str, price:float), theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str), filter_theater_id (int or None), filter_date (str or None) |
| /showtimes/select/<int:showtime_id> | select_showtime     | POST        | redirect to seat_selection.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /seat-selection/<int:showtime_id> | seat_selection      | GET         | seat_selection.html        | seat_map (list of dict: seat_id:int, row:str, column:int, seat_type:str, status:str), selected_seats (list of str seat IDs), showtime_id (int) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | booking_confirmation | GET         | booking_confirmation.html  | showtime (dict: showtime_id:int, movie_title:str, theater_name:str, date:str, time:str, price:float), selected_seats (list of str), total_price (float) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | confirm_booking      | POST        | redirect to booking_history.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /bookings                    | booking_history        | GET         | booking_history.html       | bookings (list of dict: booking_id:int, movie_title:str, booking_date:str, seats_booked:list of str, status:str) |
| /bookings/<int:booking_id>    | booking_details        | GET         | booking_details.html       | booking (dict: booking_id:int, showtime_id:int, customer_name:str, customer_email:str, booking_date:str, total_price:float, status:str, seats_booked:list of str) |
| /theaters                    | theater_information    | GET         | theater_information.html   | theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str, location:str, city:str, screens:int, facilities:str), filter_location (str or None) |

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Elements:
  - ID: dashboard-page (Div) - Container for the dashboard page.
  - ID: featured-movies (Div) - Displays featured movie recommendations.
  - ID: browse-movies-button (Button) - Navigates to movie_catalog route (movie_catalog).
  - ID: view-bookings-button (Button) - Navigates to booking_history route (booking_history).
  - ID: showtimes-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection root (redirect to /showtimes or dashboard to showtimes function).

### 2. templates/movie_catalog.html
- Page Title: Movie Catalog
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Catalog
- Elements:
  - ID: catalog-page (Div) - Container for the catalog page.
  - ID: search-input (Input) - Text field to search movies.
  - ID: genre-filter (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter movies by genre.
  - ID: movies-grid (Div) - Grid displaying movie cards.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-movie-button-{movie_id} (Button) - Button on each movie card to view details, navigates to movie_details with movie_id.

### 3. templates/movie_details.html
- Page Title: Movie Details
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Details
- Elements:
  - ID: movie-details-page (Div) - Container for movie details.
  - ID: movie-title (H1) - Displays the movie title.
  - ID: movie-director (Div) - Displays the movie director.
  - ID: movie-rating (Div) - Displays the movie rating.
  - ID: movie-description (Div) - Displays the movie description.
  - ID: select-showtime-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection for this movie.

### 4. templates/showtime_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Showtime
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Showtime
- Elements:
  - ID: showtime-page (Div) - Container for the showtime selection page.
  - ID: showtimes-list (Div) - List of available showtimes.
  - ID: theater-filter (Dropdown) - Filter showtimes by theater.
  - ID: date-filter (Input) - Filter showtimes by date.
  - Dynamic Button ID: select-showtime-button-{showtime_id} (Button) - Button to select a showtime, posts to select_showtime route.

### 5. templates/seat_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Seats
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Seats
- Elements:
  - ID: seat-selection-page (Div) - Container for seat selection.
  - ID: seat-map (Div) - Interactive seat map.
  - ID: selected-seats-display (Div) - Shows selected seats.
  - Dynamic Button ID: seat-{row}{col} (Button) - Each seat button for seat selection.
  - ID: proceed-booking-button (Button) - Proceeds to booking confirmation.

### 6. templates/booking_confirmation.html
- Page Title: Booking Confirmation
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking Confirmation
- Elements:
  - ID: confirmation-page (Div) - Container for confirmation details.
  - ID: booking-summary (Div) - Summary of the booking.
  - ID: customer-name (Input) - Input field for customer name.
  - ID: customer-email (Input) - Input field for customer email.
  - ID: confirm-booking-button (Button) - Confirms booking submission.

### 7. templates/booking_history.html
- Page Title: Booking History
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking History
- Elements:
  - ID: bookings-page (Div) - Container for booking history.
  - ID: bookings-table (Table) - Displays all bookings.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-booking-button-{booking_id} (Button) - To view individual booking details.
  - ID: status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter bookings by status.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.

### 8. templates/theater_information.html
- Page Title: Theater Information
- Main Heading (<h1>): Theater Information
- Elements:
  - ID: theater-page (Div) - Container for theater info.
  - ID: theaters-list (Div) - Displays list of theaters.
  - ID: theater-location-filter (Dropdown) - Filter theaters by location.
  - ID: facilities-display (Div) - Shows facilities of selected theater.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.


Navigation Summary:
- dashboard_page -> movie_catalog (browse-movies-button)
- dashboard_page -> booking_history (view-bookings-button)
- dashboard_page -> showtime_selection or showtimes page (showtimes-button)
- movie_catalog -> movie_details (view-movie-button-{movie_id})
- movie_details -> showtime_selection (select-showtime-button)
- showtime_selection -> seat_selection (select-showtime-button-{showtime_id})
- seat_selection -> booking_confirmation (proceed-booking-button)
- booking_confirmation -> booking_history (confirm-booking-button)
- booking_history -> booking_details (view-booking-button-{booking_id})
- booking_history -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)
- theater_information -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/movies.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date
- Description: Stores movie information.
- Example Rows:
  1|The Matrix|Lana Wachowski|Action|8.7|136|A computer hacker learns about the true nature of reality and his role in the war against its controllers.|1999-03-31
  2|Inception|Christopher Nolan|Sci-Fi|8.8|148|A skilled thief who steals corporate secrets through the use of dream-sharing technology is given the inverse task of planting an idea.|2010-07-16
  3|The Shawshank Redemption|Frank Darabont|Drama|9.3|142|Two imprisoned men bond over a number of years, finding solace and eventual redemption through acts of common decency.|1994-09-23

### 2. data/theaters.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities
- Description: Stores theater information.
- Example Rows:
  1|Cinema Max|123 Main St|New York|10|IMAX, Dolby, Wheelchair Access
  2|Galaxy Cinemas|456 Broadway|Los Angeles|8|3D, Premium Sound, Parking
  3|Starlight Theater|789 Park Ave|Chicago|6|Luxury Seating, Restaurant, VIP Lounge

### 3. data/showtimes.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats
- Description: Stores showtimes for movies at theaters.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|19:00|12.99|85
  2|1|1|2025-02-01|22:30|12.99|40
  3|2|2|2025-02-01|18:00|14.99|95

### 4. data/seats.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status
- Description: Stores seat information and booking status.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|A|1|Standard|Available
  2|1|1|A|2|Standard|Available
  3|1|1|B|5|Premium|Booked

### 5. data/bookings.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked
- Description: Stores user bookings.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|John Doe|john@example.com|2025-01-15|25.98|Confirmed|A1,A2
  2|2|Jane Smith|jane@example.com|2025-01-16|12.99|Confirmed|F10
  3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@example.com|2025-01-17|29.98|Confirmed|C3,C4

### 6. data/genres.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): genre_id|genre_name|description
- Description: Stores genre metadata.
- Example Rows:
  1|Action|Fast-paced movies with exciting sequences and combat
  2|Drama|Character-driven stories exploring complex themes
  3|Sci-Fi|Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts

---

This design specification details all Flask routes, HTML templates, and data file schemas required to enable parallel development of backend and frontend for the MovieTicketing application. All names, types, and IDs are consistent across sections.

  <title>Booking Confirmation</title>

  <h1 id="booking-confirmation-main-heading">Booking Confirmation</h1>

      <div>Theater: {{ showtime.theater_name }}</div>
      <div>Date: {{ showtime.date }}</div>
      <div>Time: {{ showtime.time }}</div>
      <div>Price: ${{ showtime.price }}</div>
      <div id="selected-seats-display">Selected Seats: {% for seat in selected_seats %}{{ seat }} {% endfor %}</div>
      <div>Total Price: ${{ total_price }}</div>
    </div>
    <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('confirm_booking', showtime_id=showtime.showtime_id) }}">
      <label for="customer-name">Name:</label>
      <input type="text" id="customer-name" name="customer_name" required>
      <label for="customer-email">Email:</label>
      <input type="email" id="customer-email" name="customer_email" required>
      <button id="confirm-booking-button" type="submit">Confirm Booking</button>
    </form>
  </div>
  <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard_page') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
</body>

=== design_spec.md ===
# MovieTicketing Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                      | Function Name          | HTTP Method | Template Rendered          | Context Variables Passed to Template                             |
|--------------------------------|------------------------|-------------|----------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------| 
| /                              | root_redirect          | GET         | N/A (redirect)             | N/A                                                             |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard_page         | GET         | dashboard.html             | featured_movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, rating:float), upcoming_releases (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies                       | movie_catalog          | GET         | movie_catalog.html         | movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, poster_url:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>        | movie_details          | GET         | movie_details.html         | movie (dict: movie_id:int, title:str, director:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, description:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>/showtimes | showtime_selection    | GET         | showtime_selection.html    | showtimes (list of dict: showtime_id:int, date:str, time:str, theater_name:str, price:float), theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str), filter_theater_id (int or None), filter_date (str or None) |
| /showtimes/select/<int:showtime_id> | select_showtime     | POST        | redirect to seat_selection.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /seat-selection/<int:showtime_id> | seat_selection      | GET         | seat_selection.html        | seat_map (list of dict: seat_id:int, row:str, column:int, seat_type:str, status:str), selected_seats (list of str seat IDs), showtime_id (int) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | booking_confirmation | GET         | booking_confirmation.html  | showtime (dict: showtime_id:int, movie_title:str, theater_name:str, date:str, time:str, price:float), selected_seats (list of str), total_price (float) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | confirm_booking      | POST        | redirect to booking_history.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /bookings                    | booking_history        | GET         | booking_history.html       | bookings (list of dict: booking_id:int, movie_title:str, booking_date:str, seats_booked:list of str, status:str) |
| /bookings/<int:booking_id>    | booking_details        | GET         | booking_details.html       | booking (dict: booking_id:int, showtime_id:int, customer_name:str, customer_email:str, booking_date:str, total_price:float, status:str, seats_booked:list of str) |
| /theaters                    | theater_information    | GET         | theater_information.html   | theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str, location:str, city:str, screens:int, facilities:str), filter_location (str or None) |

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Elements:
  - ID: dashboard-page (Div) - Container for the dashboard page.
  - ID: featured-movies (Div) - Displays featured movie recommendations.
  - ID: browse-movies-button (Button) - Navigates to movie_catalog route (movie_catalog).
  - ID: view-bookings-button (Button) - Navigates to booking_history route (booking_history).
  - ID: showtimes-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection root (redirect to /showtimes or dashboard to showtimes function).

### 2. templates/movie_catalog.html
- Page Title: Movie Catalog
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Catalog
- Elements:
  - ID: catalog-page (Div) - Container for the catalog page.
  - ID: search-input (Input) - Text field to search movies.
  - ID: genre-filter (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter movies by genre.
  - ID: movies-grid (Div) - Grid displaying movie cards.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-movie-button-{movie_id} (Button) - Button on each movie card to view details, navigates to movie_details with movie_id.

### 3. templates/movie_details.html
- Page Title: Movie Details
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Details
- Elements:
  - ID: movie-details-page (Div) - Container for movie details.
  - ID: movie-title (H1) - Displays the movie title.
  - ID: movie-director (Div) - Displays the movie director.
  - ID: movie-rating (Div) - Displays the movie rating.
  - ID: movie-description (Div) - Displays the movie description.
  - ID: select-showtime-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection for this movie.

### 4. templates/showtime_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Showtime
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Showtime
- Elements:
  - ID: showtime-page (Div) - Container for the showtime selection page.
  - ID: showtimes-list (Div) - List of available showtimes.
  - ID: theater-filter (Dropdown) - Filter showtimes by theater.
  - ID: date-filter (Input) - Filter showtimes by date.
  - Dynamic Button ID: select-showtime-button-{showtime_id} (Button) - Button to select a showtime, posts to select_showtime route.

### 5. templates/seat_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Seats
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Seats
- Elements:
  - ID: seat-selection-page (Div) - Container for seat selection.
  - ID: seat-map (Div) - Interactive seat map.
  - ID: selected-seats-display (Div) - Shows selected seats.
  - Dynamic Button ID: seat-{row}{col} (Button) - Each seat button for seat selection.
  - ID: proceed-booking-button (Button) - Proceeds to booking confirmation.

### 6. templates/booking_confirmation.html
- Page Title: Booking Confirmation
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking Confirmation
- Elements:
  - ID: confirmation-page (Div) - Container for confirmation details.
  - ID: booking-summary (Div) - Summary of the booking.
  - ID: customer-name (Input) - Input field for customer name.
  - ID: customer-email (Input) - Input field for customer email.
  - ID: confirm-booking-button (Button) - Confirms booking submission.

### 7. templates/booking_history.html
- Page Title: Booking History
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking History
- Elements:
  - ID: bookings-page (Div) - Container for booking history.
  - ID: bookings-table (Table) - Displays all bookings.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-booking-button-{booking_id} (Button) - To view individual booking details.
  - ID: status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter bookings by status.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.

### 8. templates/theater_information.html
- Page Title: Theater Information
- Main Heading (<h1>): Theater Information
- Elements:
  - ID: theater-page (Div) - Container for theater info.
  - ID: theaters-list (Div) - Displays list of theaters.
  - ID: theater-location-filter (Dropdown) - Filter theaters by location.
  - ID: facilities-display (Div) - Shows facilities of selected theater.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.


Navigation Summary:
- dashboard_page -> movie_catalog (browse-movies-button)
- dashboard_page -> booking_history (view-bookings-button)
- dashboard_page -> showtime_selection or showtimes page (showtimes-button)
- movie_catalog -> movie_details (view-movie-button-{movie_id})
- movie_details -> showtime_selection (select-showtime-button)
- showtime_selection -> seat_selection (select-showtime-button-{showtime_id})
- seat_selection -> booking_confirmation (proceed-booking-button)
- booking_confirmation -> booking_history (confirm-booking-button)
- booking_history -> booking_details (view-booking-button-{booking_id})
- booking_history -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)
- theater_information -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/movies.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date
- Description: Stores movie information.
- Example Rows:
  1|The Matrix|Lana Wachowski|Action|8.7|136|A computer hacker learns about the true nature of reality and his role in the war against its controllers.|1999-03-31
  2|Inception|Christopher Nolan|Sci-Fi|8.8|148|A skilled thief who steals corporate secrets through the use of dream-sharing technology is given the inverse task of planting an idea.|2010-07-16
  3|The Shawshank Redemption|Frank Darabont|Drama|9.3|142|Two imprisoned men bond over a number of years, finding solace and eventual redemption through acts of common decency.|1994-09-23

### 2. data/theaters.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities
- Description: Stores theater information.
- Example Rows:
  1|Cinema Max|123 Main St|New York|10|IMAX, Dolby, Wheelchair Access
  2|Galaxy Cinemas|456 Broadway|Los Angeles|8|3D, Premium Sound, Parking
  3|Starlight Theater|789 Park Ave|Chicago|6|Luxury Seating, Restaurant, VIP Lounge

### 3. data/showtimes.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats
- Description: Stores showtimes for movies at theaters.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|19:00|12.99|85
  2|1|1|2025-02-01|22:30|12.99|40
  3|2|2|2025-02-01|18:00|14.99|95

### 4. data/seats.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status
- Description: Stores seat information and booking status.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|A|1|Standard|Available
  2|1|1|A|2|Standard|Available
  3|1|1|B|5|Premium|Booked

### 5. data/bookings.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked
- Description: Stores user bookings.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|John Doe|john@example.com|2025-01-15|25.98|Confirmed|A1,A2
  2|2|Jane Smith|jane@example.com|2025-01-16|12.99|Confirmed|F10
  3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@example.com|2025-01-17|29.98|Confirmed|C3,C4

### 6. data/genres.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): genre_id|genre_name|description
- Description: Stores genre metadata.
- Example Rows:
  1|Action|Fast-paced movies with exciting sequences and combat
  2|Drama|Character-driven stories exploring complex themes
  3|Sci-Fi|Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts

---

This design specification details all Flask routes, HTML templates, and data file schemas required to enable parallel development of backend and frontend for the MovieTicketing application. All names, types, and IDs are consistent across sections.

=== design_spec.md ===
# MovieTicketing Application Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                      | Function Name          | HTTP Method | Template Rendered          | Context Variables Passed to Template                             |
|--------------------------------|------------------------|-------------|----------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------| 
| /                              | root_redirect          | GET         | N/A (redirect)             | N/A                                                             |
| /dashboard                     | dashboard_page         | GET         | dashboard.html             | featured_movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, rating:float), upcoming_releases (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies                       | movie_catalog          | GET         | movie_catalog.html         | movies (list of dict: movie_id:int, title:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, poster_url:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>        | movie_details          | GET         | movie_details.html         | movie (dict: movie_id:int, title:str, director:str, genre:str, rating:float, duration:int, description:str, release_date:str) |
| /movies/<int:movie_id>/showtimes | showtime_selection    | GET         | showtime_selection.html    | showtimes (list of dict: showtime_id:int, date:str, time:str, theater_name:str, price:float), theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str), filter_theater_id (int or None), filter_date (str or None) |
| /showtimes/select/<int:showtime_id> | select_showtime     | POST        | redirect to seat_selection.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /seat-selection/<int:showtime_id> | seat_selection      | GET         | seat_selection.html        | seat_map (list of dict: seat_id:int, row:str, column:int, seat_type:str, status:str), selected_seats (list of str seat IDs), showtime_id (int) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | booking_confirmation | GET         | booking_confirmation.html  | showtime (dict: showtime_id:int, movie_title:str, theater_name:str, date:str, time:str, price:float), selected_seats (list of str), total_price (float) |
| /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | confirm_booking      | POST        | redirect to booking_history.html (redirect) | N/A |
| /bookings                    | booking_history        | GET         | booking_history.html       | bookings (list of dict: booking_id:int, movie_title:str, booking_date:str, seats_booked:list of str, status:str) |
| /bookings/<int:booking_id>    | booking_details        | GET         | booking_details.html       | booking (dict: booking_id:int, showtime_id:int, customer_name:str, customer_email:str, booking_date:str, total_price:float, status:str, seats_booked:list of str) |
| /theaters                    | theater_information    | GET         | theater_information.html   | theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str, location:str, city:str, screens:int, facilities:str), filter_location (str or None) |

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### 1. templates/dashboard.html
- Page Title: Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Ticketing Dashboard
- Elements:
  - ID: dashboard-page (Div) - Container for the dashboard page.
  - ID: featured-movies (Div) - Displays featured movie recommendations.
  - ID: browse-movies-button (Button) - Navigates to movie_catalog route (movie_catalog).
  - ID: view-bookings-button (Button) - Navigates to booking_history route (booking_history).
  - ID: showtimes-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection root (redirect to /showtimes or dashboard to showtimes function).

### 2. templates/movie_catalog.html
- Page Title: Movie Catalog
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Catalog
- Elements:
  - ID: catalog-page (Div) - Container for the catalog page.
  - ID: search-input (Input) - Text field to search movies.
  - ID: genre-filter (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter movies by genre.
  - ID: movies-grid (Div) - Grid displaying movie cards.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-movie-button-{movie_id} (Button) - Button on each movie card to view details, navigates to movie_details with movie_id.

### 3. templates/movie_details.html
- Page Title: Movie Details
- Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Details
- Elements:
  - ID: movie-details-page (Div) - Container for movie details.
  - ID: movie-title (H1) - Displays the movie title.
  - ID: movie-director (Div) - Displays the movie director.
  - ID: movie-rating (Div) - Displays the movie rating.
  - ID: movie-description (Div) - Displays the movie description.
  - ID: select-showtime-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection for this movie.

### 4. templates/showtime_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Showtime
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Showtime
- Elements:
  - ID: showtime-page (Div) - Container for the showtime selection page.
  - ID: showtimes-list (Div) - List of available showtimes.
  - ID: theater-filter (Dropdown) - Filter showtimes by theater.
  - ID: date-filter (Input) - Filter showtimes by date.
  - Dynamic Button ID: select-showtime-button-{showtime_id} (Button) - Button to select a showtime, posts to select_showtime route.

### 5. templates/seat_selection.html
- Page Title: Select Seats
- Main Heading (<h1>): Select Seats
- Elements:
  - ID: seat-selection-page (Div) - Container for seat selection.
  - ID: seat-map (Div) - Interactive seat map.
  - ID: selected-seats-display (Div) - Shows selected seats.
  - Dynamic Button ID: seat-{row}{col} (Button) - Each seat button for seat selection.
  - ID: proceed-booking-button (Button) - Proceeds to booking confirmation.

### 6. templates/booking_confirmation.html
- Page Title: Booking Confirmation
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking Confirmation
- Elements:
  - ID: confirmation-page (Div) - Container for confirmation details.
  - ID: booking-summary (Div) - Summary of the booking.
  - ID: customer-name (Input) - Input field for customer name.
  - ID: customer-email (Input) - Input field for customer email.
  - ID: confirm-booking-button (Button) - Confirms booking submission.

### 7. templates/booking_history.html
- Page Title: Booking History
- Main Heading (<h1>): Booking History
- Elements:
  - ID: bookings-page (Div) - Container for booking history.
  - ID: bookings-table (Table) - Displays all bookings.
  - Dynamic Button ID: view-booking-button-{booking_id} (Button) - To view individual booking details.
  - ID: status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter bookings by status.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.

### 8. templates/theater_information.html
- Page Title: Theater Information
- Main Heading (<h1>): Theater Information
- Elements:
  - ID: theater-page (Div) - Container for theater info.
  - ID: theaters-list (Div) - Displays list of theaters.
  - ID: theater-location-filter (Dropdown) - Filter theaters by location.
  - ID: facilities-display (Div) - Shows facilities of selected theater.
  - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.


Navigation Summary:
- dashboard_page -> movie_catalog (browse-movies-button)
- dashboard_page -> booking_history (view-bookings-button)
- dashboard_page -> showtime_selection or showtimes page (showtimes-button)
- movie_catalog -> movie_details (view-movie-button-{movie_id})
- movie_details -> showtime_selection (select-showtime-button)
- showtime_selection -> seat_selection (select-showtime-button-{showtime_id})
- seat_selection -> booking_confirmation (proceed-booking-button)
- booking_confirmation -> booking_history (confirm-booking-button)
- booking_history -> booking_details (view-booking-button-{booking_id})
- booking_history -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)
- theater_information -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. data/movies.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date
- Description: Stores movie information.
- Example Rows:
  1|The Matrix|Lana Wachowski|Action|8.7|136|A computer hacker learns about the true nature of reality and his role in the war against its controllers.|1999-03-31
  2|Inception|Christopher Nolan|Sci-Fi|8.8|148|A skilled thief who steals corporate secrets through the use of dream-sharing technology is given the inverse task of planting an idea.|2010-07-16
  3|The Shawshank Redemption|Frank Darabont|Drama|9.3|142|Two imprisoned men bond over a number of years, finding solace and eventual redemption through acts of common decency.|1994-09-23

### 2. data/theaters.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities
- Description: Stores theater information.
- Example Rows:
  1|Cinema Max|123 Main St|New York|10|IMAX, Dolby, Wheelchair Access
  2|Galaxy Cinemas|456 Broadway|Los Angeles|8|3D, Premium Sound, Parking
  3|Starlight Theater|789 Park Ave|Chicago|6|Luxury Seating, Restaurant, VIP Lounge

### 3. data/showtimes.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats
- Description: Stores showtimes for movies at theaters.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|19:00|12.99|85
  2|1|1|2025-02-01|22:30|12.99|40
  3|2|2|2025-02-01|18:00|14.99|95

### 4. data/seats.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status
- Description: Stores seat information and booking status.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|1|A|1|Standard|Available
  2|1|1|A|2|Standard|Available
  3|1|1|B|5|Premium|Booked

### 5. data/bookings.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked
- Description: Stores user bookings.
- Example Rows:
  1|1|John Doe|john@example.com|2025-01-15|25.98|Confirmed|A1,A2
  2|2|Jane Smith|jane@example.com|2025-01-16|12.99|Confirmed|F10
  3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@example.com|2025-01-17|29.98|Confirmed|C3,C4

### 6. data/genres.txt
- Fields (pipe-delimited): genre_id|genre_name|description
- Description: Stores genre metadata.
- Example Rows:
  1|Action|Fast-paced movies with exciting sequences and combat
  2|Drama|Character-driven stories exploring complex themes
  3|Sci-Fi|Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts

---

This design specification details all Flask routes, HTML templates, and data file schemas required to enable parallel development of backend and frontend for the MovieTicketing application. All names, types, and IDs are consistent across sections.

/showtimes/select/<int:showtime_id> | select_showtime     | POST        | redirect to seat_selection.html (redirect) | N/A | | /seat-selection/<int:showtime_id> | seat_selection      | GET         | seat_selection.html        | seat_map (list of dict: seat_id:int, row:str, column:int, seat_type:str, status:str), selected_seats (list of str seat IDs), showtime_id (int) | | /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | booking_confirmation | GET         | booking_confirmation.html  | showtime (dict: showtime_id:int, movie_title:str, theater_name:str, date:str, time:str, price:float), selected_seats (list of str), total_price (float) | | /booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id> | confirm_booking      | POST        | redirect to booking_history.html (redirect) | N/A | | /bookings                    | booking_history        | GET         | booking_history.html       | bookings (list of dict: booking_id:int, movie_title:str, booking_date:str, seats_booked:list of str, status:str) | | /bookings/<int:booking_id>    | booking_details        | GET         | booking_details.html       | booking (dict: booking_id:int, showtime_id:int, customer_name:str, customer_email:str, booking_date:str, total_price:float, status:str, seats_booked:list of str) | | /theaters                    | theater_information    | GET         | theater_information.html   | theaters (list of dict: theater_id:int, theater_name:str, location:str, city:str, screens:int, facilities:str), filter_location (str or None) |  ---  ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications  ### 1. templates/dashboard.html - Page Title: Movie Ticketing Dashboard - Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Ticketing Dashboard - Elements:   - ID: dashboard-page (Div) - Container for the dashboard page.   - ID: featured-movies (Div) - Displays featured movie recommendations.   - ID: browse-movies-button (Button) - Navigates to movie_catalog route (movie_catalog).   - ID: view-bookings-button (Button) - Navigates to booking_history route (booking_history).   - ID: showtimes-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection root (redirect to /showtimes or dashboard to showtimes function).  ### 2. templates/movie_catalog.html - Page Title: Movie Catalog - Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Catalog - Elements:   - ID: catalog-page (Div) - Container for the catalog page.   - ID: search-input (Input) - Text field to search movies.   - ID: genre-filter (Dropdown) - Dropdown to filter movies by genre.   - ID: movies-grid (Div) - Grid displaying movie cards.   - Dynamic Button ID: view-movie-button-{movie_id} (Button) - Button on each movie card to view details, navigates to movie_details with movie_id.  ### 3. templates/movie_details.html - Page Title: Movie Details - Main Heading (<h1>): Movie Details - Elements:   - ID: movie-details-page (Div) - Container for movie details.   - ID: movie-title (H1) - Displays the movie title.   - ID: movie-director (Div) - Displays the movie director.   - ID: movie-rating (Div) - Displays the movie rating.   - ID: movie-description (Div) - Displays the movie description.   - ID: select-showtime-button (Button) - Navigates to showtime_selection for this movie.  ### 4. templates/showtime_selection.html - Page Title: Select Showtime - Main Heading (<h1>): Select Showtime - Elements:   - ID: showtime-page (Div) - Container for the showtime selection page.   - ID: showtimes-list (Div) - List of available showtimes.   - ID: theater-filter (Dropdown) - Filter showtimes by theater.   - ID: date-filter (Input) - Filter showtimes by date.   - Dynamic Button ID: select-showtime-button-{showtime_id} (Button) - Button to select a showtime, posts to select_showtime route.  ### 5. templates/seat_selection.html - Page Title: Select Seats - Main Heading (<h1>): Select Seats - Elements:   - ID: seat-selection-page (Div) - Container for seat selection.   - ID: seat-map (Div) - Interactive seat map.   - ID: selected-seats-display (Div) - Shows selected seats.   - Dynamic Button ID: seat-{row}{col} (Button) - Each seat button for seat selection.   - ID: proceed-booking-button (Button) - Proceeds to booking confirmation.  ### 6. templates/booking_confirmation.html - Page Title: Booking Confirmation - Main Heading (<h1>): Booking Confirmation - Elements:   - ID: confirmation-page (Div) - Container for confirmation details.   - ID: booking-summary (Div) - Summary of the booking.   - ID: customer-name (Input) - Input field for customer name.   - ID: customer-email (Input) - Input field for customer email.   - ID: confirm-booking-button (Button) - Confirms booking submission.  ### 7. templates/booking_history.html - Page Title: Booking History - Main Heading (<h1>): Booking History - Elements:   - ID: bookings-page (Div) - Container for booking history.   - ID: bookings-table (Table) - Displays all bookings.   - Dynamic Button ID: view-booking-button-{booking_id} (Button) - To view individual booking details.   - ID: status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter bookings by status.   - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.  ### 8. templates/theater_information.html - Page Title: Theater Information - Main Heading (<h1>): Theater Information - Elements:   - ID: theater-page (Div) - Container for theater info.   - ID: theaters-list (Div) - Displays list of theaters.   - ID: theater-location-filter (Dropdown) - Filter theaters by location.   - ID: facilities-display (Div) - Shows facilities of selected theater.   - ID: back-to-dashboard (Button) - Navigates back to dashboard.   Navigation Summary: - dashboard_page -> movie_catalog (browse-movies-button) - dashboard_page -> booking_history (view-bookings-button) - dashboard_page -> showtime_selection or showtimes page (showtimes-button) - movie_catalog -> movie_details (view-movie-button-{movie_id}) - movie_details -> showtime_selection (select-showtime-button) - showtime_selection -> seat_selection (select-showtime-button-{showtime_id}) - seat_selection -> booking_confirmation (proceed-booking-button) - booking_confirmation -> booking_history (confirm-booking-button) - booking_history -> booking_details (view-booking-button-{booking_id}) - booking_history -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard) - theater_information -> dashboard_page (back-to-dashboard)  ---  ## Section 3: Data File Schemas  ### 1. data/movies.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date - Description: Stores movie information. - Example Rows:   1|The Matrix|Lana Wachowski|Action|8.7|136|A computer hacker learns about the true nature of reality and his role in the war against its controllers.|1999-03-31   2|Inception|Christopher Nolan|Sci-Fi|8.8|148|A skilled thief who steals corporate secrets through the use of dream-sharing technology is given the inverse task of planting an idea.|2010-07-16   3|The Shawshank Redemption|Frank Darabont|Drama|9.3|142|Two imprisoned men bond over a number of years, finding solace and eventual redemption through acts of common decency.|1994-09-23  ### 2. data/theaters.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities - Description: Stores theater information. - Example Rows:   1|Cinema Max|123 Main St|New York|10|IMAX, Dolby, Wheelchair Access   2|Galaxy Cinemas|456 Broadway|Los Angeles|8|3D, Premium Sound, Parking   3|Starlight Theater|789 Park Ave|Chicago|6|Luxury Seating, Restaurant, VIP Lounge  ### 3. data/showtimes.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats - Description: Stores showtimes for movies at theaters. - Example Rows:   1|1|1|2025-02-01|19:00|12.99|85   2|1|1|2025-02-01|22:30|12.99|40   3|2|2|2025-02-01|18:00|14.99|95  ### 4. data/seats.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status - Description: Stores seat information and booking status. - Example Rows:   1|1|1|A|1|Standard|Available   2|1|1|A|2|Standard|Available   3|1|1|B|5|Premium|Booked  ### 5. data/bookings.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked - Description: Stores user bookings. - Example Rows:   1|1|John Doe|john@example.com|2025-01-15|25.98|Confirmed|A1,A2   2|2|Jane Smith|jane@example.com|2025-01-16|12.99|Confirmed|F10   3|3|Robert Johnson|robert@example.com|2025-01-17|29.98|Confirmed|C3,C4  ### 6. data/genres.txt - Fields (pipe-delimited): genre_id|genre_name|description - Description: Stores genre metadata. - Example Rows:   1|Action|Fast-paced movies with exciting sequences and combat   2|Drama|Character-driven stories exploring complex themes   3|Sci-Fi|Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts  ---  This design specification details all Flask routes, HTML templates, and data file schemas required to enable parallel development of backend and frontend for the MovieTicketing application. All names, types, and IDs are consistent across sections.

[Tool_Request] BackendDeveloper_Failover: write_text_file({"filename":"app.py","content":"from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, abort\nimport os\nfrom typing import List, Dict\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\napp.secret_key = \"your_secret_key\"\n\nDATA_DIR = \"data\"\nMOVIES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \"movies.txt\")\nTHEATERS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \"theaters.txt\")\nSHOWTIMES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \"showtimes.txt\")\nSEATS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \"seats.txt\")\nBOOKINGS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \"bookings.txt\")\nGENRES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \"genres.txt\")\n\n\ndef load_pipe_delimited(filepath: str, expected_columns: int) -> List[List[str]]:\n    rows = []\n    if not os.path.exists(filepath):\n        return rows\n    try:\n        with open(filepath, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            for line in f:\n                line = line.strip()\n                if not line:\n                    continue\n                parts = line.split(\"|\")\n                if len(parts) == expected_columns:\n                    rows.append(parts)\n        return rows\n    except Exception:\n        return []\n\n\ndef load_movies() -> List[Dict]:\n    # movie_id|title|director|genre|rating|duration|description|release_date\n    raw = load_pipe_delimited(MOVIES_FILE, 8)\n    movies = []\n    for r in raw:\n        try:\n            movies.append({\n                \"movie_id\": int(r[0]),\n                \"title\": r[1],\n                \"director\": r[2],\n                \"genre\": r[3],\n                \"rating\": float(r[4]),\n                \"duration\": int(r[5]),\n                \"description\": r[6],\n                \"release_date\": r[7]\n            })\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return movies\n\n\ndef load_theaters() -> List[Dict]:\n    # theater_id|theater_name|location|city|screens|facilities\n    raw = load_pipe_delimited(THEATERS_FILE, 6)\n    theaters = []\n    for r in raw:\n        try:\n            theaters.append({\n                \"theater_id\": int(r[0]),\n                \"theater_name\": r[1],\n                \"location\": r[2],\n                \"city\": r[3],\n                \"screens\": int(r[4]),\n                \"facilities\": r[5]  # raw string like: \"3D, Premium Parking\"\n            })\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return theaters\n\n\ndef load_showtimes() -> List[Dict]:\n    # showtime_id|movie_id|theater_id|showtime_date|showtime_time|price|available_seats\n    raw = load_pipe_delimited(SHOWTIMES_FILE, 7)\n    showtimes = []\n    for r in raw:\n        try:\n            showtimes.append({\n                \"showtime_id\": int(r[0]),\n                \"movie_id\": int(r[1]),\n                \"theater_id\": int(r[2]),\n                \"date\": r[3],\n                \"time\": r[4],\n                \"price\": float(r[5]),\n                \"available_seats\": int(r[6])\n            })\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return showtimes\n\n\ndef load_seats() -> List[Dict]:\n    # seat_id|theater_id|screen_id|row|column|seat_type|status\n    raw = load_pipe_delimited(SEATS_FILE, 7)\n    seats = []\n    for r in raw:\n        try:\n            seats.append({\n                \"seat_id\": int(r[0]),\n                \"theater_id\": int(r[1]),\n                \"screen_id\": int(r[2]),\n                \"row\": r[3],\n                \"column\": int(r[4]),\n                \"seat_type\": r[5],\n                \"status\": r[6]  # Available or Booked\n            })\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return seats\n\n\ndef save_seats(seats: List[Dict]):\n    try:\n        with open(SEATS_FILE, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            for seat in seats:\n                line = f\"{seat['seat_id']}|{seat['theater_id']}|{seat['screen_id']}|{seat['row']}|{seat['column']}|{seat['seat_type']}|{seat['status']}\\n\"\n                f.write(line)\n        return True\n    except Exception:\n        return False\n\n\ndef load_bookings() -> List[Dict]:\n    # booking_id|showtime_id|customer_name|customer_email|booking_date|total_price|status|seats_booked\n    raw = load_pipe_delimited(BOOKINGS_FILE, 8)\n    bookings = []\n    for r in raw:\n        try:\n            bookings.append({\n                \"booking_id\": int(r[0]),\n                \"showtime_id\": int(r[1]),\n                \"customer_name\": r[2],\n                \"customer_email\": r[3],\n                \"booking_date\": r[4],\n                \"total_price\": float(r[5]),\n                \"status\": r[6],\n                \"seats_booked\": r[7].split(\",\") if r[7] else []\n            })\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return bookings\n\n\ndef save_bookings(bookings: List[Dict]) -> bool:\n    try:\n        with open(BOOKINGS_FILE, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            for b in bookings:\n                seats_str = \",\".join(b[\"seats_booked\"])\n                line = f\"{b['booking_id']}|{b['showtime_id']}|{b['customer_name']}|{b['customer_email']}|{b['booking_date']}|{b['total_price']:.2f}|{b['status']}|{seats_str}\\n\"\n                f.write(line)\n        return True\n    except Exception:\n        return False\n\n\ndef load_genres() -> List[Dict]:\n    # genre_id|genre_name|description\n    raw = load_pipe_delimited(GENRES_FILE, 3)\n    genres = []\n    for r in raw:\n        try:\n            genres.append({\n                \"genre_id\": int(r[0]),\n                \"genre_name\": r[1],\n                \"description\": r[2]\n            })\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    return genres\n\n\n@app.route(\"/\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef root_redirect():\n    return redirect(url_for(\"dashboard_page\"))\n\n\n@app.route(\"/dashboard\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef dashboard_page():\n    movies = load_movies()\n    # Featured movies: top rated (top 5) by rating descending\n    movies_sorted = sorted(movies, key=lambda m: m[\"rating\"], reverse=True)\n    featured_movies = [{\"movie_id\": m[\"movie_id\"], \"title\": m[\"title\"], \"rating\": m[\"rating\"]} for m in movies_sorted[:5]]\n\n    # Upcoming releases: sort by release_date ascending, next 5 upcoming from today (simple filter)\n    today_str = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d\")\n    upcoming = [m for m in movies if m[\"release_date\"] >= today_str]\n    upcoming_releases_sorted = sorted(upcoming, key=lambda m: m[\"release_date\"])\n    upcoming_releases = [{\"movie_id\": m[\"movie_id\"], \"title\": m[\"title\"], \"release_date\": m[\"release_date\"]} for m in upcoming_releases_sorted[:5]]\n\n    return render_template(\"dashboard.html\", featured_movies=featured_movies, upcoming_releases=upcoming_releases)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/movies\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef movie_catalog():\n    movies = load_movies()\n    genres = load_genres()\n    # Add poster_url as static path /static/posters/{movie_id}.jpg\n    movies_context = []\n    for m in movies:\n        movies_context.append({\n            \"movie_id\": m[\"movie_id\"],\n            \"title\": m[\"title\"],\n            \"genre\": m[\"genre\"],\n            \"rating\": m[\"rating\"],\n            \"duration\": m[\"duration\"],\n            \"poster_url\": url_for('static', filename=f\"posters/{m['movie_id']}.jpg\")\n        })\n    return render_template(\"movie_catalog.html\", movies=movies_context, genres=genres)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/movies/<int:movie_id>\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef movie_details(movie_id: int):\n    movies = load_movies()\n    movie = next((m for m in movies if m[\"movie_id\"] == movie_id), None)\n    if not movie:\n        abort(404)\n    return render_template(\"movie_details.html\", movie=movie)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/movies/<int:movie_id>/showtimes\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef showtime_selection(movie_id: int):\n    theaters = load_theaters()\n    showtimes_all = load_showtimes()\n\n    # Filters\n    filter_theater_id = request.args.get(\"filter_theater_id\", type=int)\n    filter_date = request.args.get(\"filter_date\", default=None, type=str)\n\n    # Filter showtimes for given movie\n    showtimes_filtered = [s for s in showtimes_all if s[\"movie_id\"] == movie_id]\n\n    if filter_theater_id is not None:\n        showtimes_filtered = [s for s in showtimes_filtered if s[\"theater_id\"] == filter_theater_id]\n    if filter_date:\n        showtimes_filtered = [s for s in showtimes_filtered if s[\"date\"] == filter_date]\n\n    # Build list of showtime dicts with theater_name\n    theater_map = {t[\"theater_id\"]: t for t in theaters}\n    showtimes_context = []\n    for s in showtimes_filtered:\n        t = theater_map.get(s[\"theater_id\"])\n        if not t:\n            continue\n        showtimes_context.append({\n            \"showtime_id\": s[\"showtime_id\"],\n            \"date\": s[\"date\"],\n            \"time\": s[\"time\"],\n            \"theater_name\": t[\"theater_name\"],\n            \"price\": s[\"price\"]\n        })\n\n    theaters_context = [{\"theater_id\": t[\"theater_id\"], \"theater_name\": t[\"theater_name\"]} for t in theaters]\n\n    return render_template(\"showtime_selection.html\", showtimes=showtimes_context, theaters=theaters_context,\n                           filter_theater_id=filter_theater_id, filter_date=filter_date)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/showtimes/select/<int:showtime_id>\", methods=[\"POST\"])\ndef select_showtime(showtime_id: int):\n    # Redirect to seat selection page\n    return redirect(url_for(\"seat_selection\", showtime_id=showtime_id))\n\n\n@app.route(\"/seat-selection/<int:showtime_id>\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef seat_selection(showtime_id: int):\n    showtimes = load_showtimes()\n    st = next((s for s in showtimes if s[\"showtime_id\"] == showtime_id), None)\n    if not st:\n        abort(404)\n\n    seats = load_seats()\n    # Filter seats for theater and screen of the showtime\n    relevant_seats = [seat for seat in seats if seat[\"theater_id\"] == st[\"theater_id\"]]\n\n    seat_map = []\n    for seat in relevant_seats:\n        # Compose seat dict with required fields\n        seat_map.append({\n            \"seat_id\": seat[\"seat_id\"],\n            \"row\": seat[\"row\"],\n            \"column\": seat[\"column\"],\n            \"seat_type\": seat[\"seat_type\"],\n            \"status\": seat[\"status\"]\n        })\n\n    selected_seats = []  # Initially empty\n\n    return render_template(\"seat_selection.html\", seat_map=seat_map, selected_seats=selected_seats, showtime_id=showtime_id)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/booking/confirm/<int:showtime_id>\", methods=[\"GET\", \"POST\"])\ndef booking_confirmation(showtime_id: int):\n    showtimes = load_showtimes()\n    theaters = load_theaters()\n    movies = load_movies()\n\n    st = next((s for s in showtimes if s[\"showtime_id\"] == showtime_id), None)\n    if not st:\n        abort(404)\n    theater = next((t for t in theaters if t[\"theater_id\"] == st[\"theater_id\"]), None)\n    movie = next((m for m in movies if m[\"movie_id\"] == st[\"movie_id\"]), None)\n    if not theater or not movie:\n        abort(404)\n\n    if request.method == \"GET\":\n        selected_seats = request.args.getlist(\"selected_seats\")\n        total_price = st[\"price\"] * len(selected_seats)\n\n        showtime_context = {\n            \"showtime_id\": showtime_id,\n            \"movie_title\": movie[\"title\"],\n            \"theater_name\": theater[\"theater_name\"],\n            \"date\": st[\"date\"],\n            \"time\": st[\"time\"],\n            \"price\": st[\"price\"]\n        }\n        return render_template(\"booking_confirmation.html\", showtime=showtime_context,\n                               selected_seats=selected_seats, total_price=total_price)\n    else:\n        # POST to confirm booking\n        customer_name = request.form.get(\"customer-name\", \"\").strip()\n        customer_email = request.form.get(\"customer-email\", \"\").strip()\n        selected_seats = request.form.getlist(\"selected_seats\")\n\n        if not customer_name or not customer_email or not selected_seats:\n            abort(400)\n\n        total_price = st[\"price\"] * len(selected_seats)\n        bookings = load_bookings()\n        max_booking_id = max([b[\"booking_id\"] for b in bookings], default=0)\n        new_booking_id = max_booking_id + 1\n        booking_date = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d\")\n\n        new_booking = {\n            \"booking_id\": new_booking_id,\n            \"showtime_id\": showtime_id,\n            \"customer_name\": customer_name,\n            \"customer_email\": customer_email,\n            \"booking_date\": booking_date,\n            \"total_price\": total_price,\n            \"status\": \"Confirmed\",\n            \"seats_booked\": selected_seats\n        }\n\n        bookings.append(new_booking)\n\n        if not save_bookings(bookings):\n            abort(500)\n\n        # Update seat status to Booked\n        seats = load_seats()\n        seat_id_set = set()\n        # We do not have seat_ids as strings from form, convert from IDs as str to int\n        try:\n            seat_id_set = set(int(s) for s in selected_seats)\n        except Exception:\n            abort(400)\n\n        changed = False\n        for seat in seats:\n            if seat[\"seat_id\"] in seat_id_set:\n                if seat[\"status\"] == \"Available\":\n                    seat[\"status\"] = \"Booked\"\n                    changed = True\n\n        if changed:\n            if not save_seats(seats):\n                # Could not save seat updates but booking saved\n                pass\n\n        return redirect(url_for(\"booking_history\"))\n\n\n@app.route(\"/bookings\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef booking_history():\n    bookings = load_bookings()\n    showtimes = load_showtimes()\n    movies = load_movies()\n\n    showtime_map = {s[\"showtime_id\"]: s for s in showtimes}\n    movie_map = {m[\"movie_id\"]: m for m in movies}\n\n    bookings_context = []\n    for b in bookings:\n        st = showtime_map.get(b[\"showtime_id\"])\n        movie_title = \"Unknown\"\n        if st:\n            movie = movie_map.get(st[\"movie_id\"])\n            if movie:\n                movie_title = movie[\"title\"]\n\n        bookings_context.append({\n            \"booking_id\": b[\"booking_id\"],\n            \"movie_title\": movie_title,\n            \"booking_date\": b[\"booking_date\"],\n            \"seats_booked\": b[\"seats_booked\"],\n            \"status\": b[\"status\"]\n        })\n\n    return render_template(\"booking_history.html\", bookings=bookings_context)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/bookings/<int:booking_id>\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef booking_details(booking_id: int):\n    bookings = load_bookings()\n    booking = next((b for b in bookings if b[\"booking_id\"] == booking_id), None)\n    if not booking:\n        abort(404)\n    return render_template(\"booking_details.html\", booking=booking)\n\n\n@app.route(\"/theaters\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef theater_information():\n    filter_location = request.args.get(\"filter_location\", default=None, type=str)\n    theaters = load_theaters()\n    if filter_location:\n        theaters = [t for t in theaters if filter_location.lower() in t[\"location\"].lower()]\n\n    return render_template(\"theater_information.html\", theaters=theaters, filter_location=filter_location)\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    app.run()\n"})
